###House Lannister#### 
#####Hear me Roar#####

#Lannisters Ancient History.
#Just updated some things. I got to a chapter in AFoC were Jaime is speaking to his aunt. It's stated that Tytos was third-born.
#So rather than mess with his younger brothers Damon (Joanna's dad) and Damion (Lannisport Lannisters). 
#I've added two elder brothers to them all, who died childless. Added random wives for Damon so Tybolt and Tya are full siblings and one to Tybolt so his five sons are full blooded too.

###A Lannister always pays his debt###
###Lann the Clever, founder of House Lannister###

16199 = {		
	name="Hodor" # One of the Regents of Aegon III
	dynasty=199	# Westerling
	
	
	religion="the_seven"	
	culture="westerman"
	
	father=17199 # Regenard Westerling
	mother=25199
	
	add_trait="proud"	
	
	8107.1.1 = {birth="8107.1.1"}
	8123.1.1 = {add_trait="knight"}
	8129.4.1={ #Dance of the Dragons
		effect = {
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
			set_character_flag = against_king
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						tier = COUNT
						tier = DUKE
					}
				}				
				set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 9 } #westerlands
			}
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
						years = 20
					}
				}
			}
			d_dragonstone = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { year = 8130 } }
						ROOT = {
							join_attacker_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8130.1.1={ 
		effect = {
			k_westerlands = {
				holder_scope = {
					ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV }
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = { 
					remove_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			d_dragonstone = {
				holder_scope = { 
					remove_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_remove_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8133.6.1 = {
		add_trait=ill
		death= {death_reason = death_trait}
	} 
}

303229 = {
	name="Hodor"	# a lord
	dynasty=229

	religion="the_seven"
	culture="westerman"

	father=300229
	mother=400229

	7996.1.1 = {birth="7996.1.1"}
	8012.1.1 = {add_trait=knight add_trait=poor_warrior}
	8014.1.1 = {add_spouse=403229}
	8040.1.1 = {give_nickname = nick_fighting_fool}
	8043.1.1={ #Faith Militant Uprising
		effect = {
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
			set_character_flag = against_king
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						tier = COUNT
						tier = DUKE
					}
				}				
				set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 9 } #westerlands
			}
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
						years = 20
					}
				}
			}
			k_the_most_devout = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { year = 8197 } }
						ROOT = {
							join_attacker_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8044.1.1={ 
		effect = {
			d_crakehall = {
				holder_scope = {
					ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV }
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = { 
					remove_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			k_the_most_devout = {
				holder_scope = { 
					remove_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_remove_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8049.1.1 = {death="8049.1.1"}
}
